\DoxyCodeLine{03580\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ you\ decide\ what\ you\ want\ to\ use\ and\ what\ you\ want\ to\ provide.\ There\ are\ three}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03581\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ different\ ways\ to\ use\ the\ font\ atlas.\ The\ first\ two\ will\ use\ your\ font}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03588\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ So\ first\ up\ the\ easiest\ way\ to\ do\ font\ handling\ is\ by\ just\ providing\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03589\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ `nk\_user\_font`\ struct\ which\ only\ requires\ the\ height\ in\ pixel\ of\ the\ used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03590\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ font\ and\ a\ callback\ to\ calculate\ the\ width\ of\ a\ string.\ This\ way\ of\ handling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03591\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ fonts\ is\ best\ fitted\ for\ using\ the\ normal\ draw\ shape\ command\ API\ where\ you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03592\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ do\ all\ the\ text\ drawing\ yourself\ and\ the\ library\ does\ not\ require\ any\ kind}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03593\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ of\ deeper\ knowledge\ about\ which\ font\ handling\ mechanism\ you\ use.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03653\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ 3.)\ Nuklear\ font\ baker}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03654\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03655\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ The\ final\ approach\ if\ you\ do\ not\ have\ a\ font\ handling\ functionality\ or\ don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03656\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ want\ to\ use\ it\ in\ this\ library\ is\ by\ using\ the\ optional\ font\ baker.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03657\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ The\ font\ baker\ APIs\ can\ be\ used\ to\ create\ a\ font\ plus\ font\ atlas\ texture}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03658\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ and\ can\ be\ used\ with\ or\ without\ the\ vertex\ buffer\ output.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03659\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03660\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ It\ still\ uses\ the\ `nk\_user\_font`\ struct\ and\ the\ two\ different\ approaches}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03661\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ previously\ stated\ still\ work.\ The\ font\ baker\ is\ not\ located\ inside}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03662\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ `nk\_context`\ like\ all\ other\ systems\ since\ it\ can\ be\ understood\ as\ more\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03663\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ an\ extension\ to\ nuklear\ and\ does\ not\ really\ depend\ on\ any\ `nk\_context`\ state.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03664\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03665\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ Font\ baker\ need\ to\ be\ initialized\ first\ by\ one\ of\ the\ nk\_font\_atlas\_init\_xxx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03666\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ functions.\ If\ you\ don't\ care\ about\ memory\ just\ call\ the\ default\ version}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03667\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ `nk\_font\_atlas\_init\_default`\ which\ will\ allocate\ all\ memory\ from\ the\ standard\ library.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03668\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ If\ you\ want\ to\ control\ memory\ allocation\ but\ you\ don't\ care\ if\ the\ allocated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03669\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ memory\ is\ temporary\ and\ therefore\ can\ be\ freed\ directly\ after\ the\ baking\ process}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03670\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ is\ over\ or\ permanent\ you\ can\ call\ `nk\_font\_atlas\_init`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03671\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03672\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ After\ successfully\ initializing\ the\ font\ baker\ you\ can\ add\ Truetype(.ttf)\ fonts\ from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03673\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ different\ sources\ like\ memory\ or\ from\ file\ by\ calling\ one\ of\ the\ `nk\_font\_atlas\_add\_xxx`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03674\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ functions.\ Adding\ font\ will\ permanently\ store\ each\ font,\ font\ config\ and\ ttf\ memory\ block(!)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03675\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ inside\ the\ font\ atlas\ and\ allows\ to\ reuse\ the\ font\ atlas.\ If\ you\ don't\ want\ to\ reuse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03676\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ the\ font\ baker\ by\ for\ example\ adding\ additional\ fonts\ you\ can\ call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03677\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ `nk\_font\_atlas\_cleanup`\ after\ the\ baking\ process\ is\ over\ (after\ calling\ nk\_font\_atlas\_end).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03678\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03679\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ As\ soon\ as\ you\ added\ all\ fonts\ you\ wanted\ you\ can\ now\ start\ the\ baking\ process}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03680\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ for\ every\ selected\ glyph\ to\ image\ by\ calling\ `nk\_font\_atlas\_bake`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03681\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ The\ baking\ process\ returns\ image\ memory,\ width\ and\ height\ which\ can\ be\ used\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03682\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ either\ create\ your\ own\ image\ object\ or\ upload\ it\ to\ any\ graphics\ library.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03683\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ No\ matter\ which\ case\ you\ finally\ have\ to\ call\ `nk\_font\_atlas\_end`\ which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03684\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ will\ free\ all\ temporary\ memory\ including\ the\ font\ atlas\ image\ so\ make\ sure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03685\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ you\ created\ our\ texture\ beforehand.\ `nk\_font\_atlas\_end`\ requires\ a\ handle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03686\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ to\ your\ font\ texture\ or\ object\ and\ optionally\ fills\ a\ `struct\ nk\_draw\_null\_texture`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03687\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ which\ can\ be\ used\ for\ the\ optional\ vertex\ output.\ If\ you\ don't\ want\ it\ just}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03688\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ set\ the\ argument\ to\ `NULL`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03689\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03690\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ At\ this\ point\ you\ are\ done\ and\ if\ you\ don't\ want\ to\ reuse\ the\ font\ atlas\ you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03691\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ can\ call\ `nk\_font\_atlas\_cleanup`\ to\ free\ all\ truetype\ blobs\ and\ configuration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03692\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ memory.\ Finally\ if\ you\ don't\ use\ the\ font\ atlas\ and\ any\ of\ it's\ fonts\ anymore}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03693\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ you\ need\ to\ call\ `nk\_font\_atlas\_clear`\ to\ free\ all\ memory\ still\ being\ used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03694\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03695\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ struct\ nk\_font\_atlas\ atlas;}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03892\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ \ A\ basic\ (double)-\/buffer\ with\ linear\ allocation\ and\ resetting\ as\ only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03893\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ freeing\ policy.\ The\ buffer's\ main\ purpose\ is\ to\ control\ all\ memory\ management}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03894\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ inside\ the\ GUI\ toolkit\ and\ still\ leave\ memory\ control\ as\ much\ as\ possible\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03895\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ the\ hand\ of\ the\ user\ while\ also\ making\ sure\ the\ library\ is\ easy\ to\ use\ if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03896\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ not\ as\ much\ control\ is\ needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03897\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ In\ general\ all\ memory\ inside\ this\ library\ can\ be\ provided\ from\ the\ user\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03898\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ three\ different\ ways.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03899\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03900\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ The\ first\ way\ and\ the\ one\ providing\ most\ control\ is\ by\ just\ passing\ a\ fixed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03901\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ size\ memory\ block.\ In\ this\ case\ all\ control\ lies\ in\ the\ hand\ of\ the\ user}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03902\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ since\ he\ can\ exactly\ control\ where\ the\ memory\ comes\ from\ and\ how\ much\ memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03903\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ the\ library\ should\ consume.\ Of\ course\ using\ the\ fixed\ size\ API\ removes\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03904\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ ability\ to\ automatically\ resize\ a\ buffer\ if\ not\ enough\ memory\ is\ provided\ so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03905\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ you\ have\ to\ take\ over\ the\ resizing.\ While\ being\ a\ fixed\ sized\ buffer\ sounds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03906\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ quite\ limiting,\ it\ is\ very\ effective\ in\ this\ library\ since\ the\ actual\ memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03907\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ consumption\ is\ quite\ stable\ and\ has\ a\ fixed\ upper\ bound\ for\ a\ lot\ of\ cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03908\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03909\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ If\ you\ don't\ want\ to\ think\ about\ how\ much\ memory\ the\ library\ should\ allocate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03910\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ at\ all\ time\ or\ have\ a\ very\ dynamic\ UI\ with\ unpredictable\ memory\ consumption}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03911\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ habits\ but\ still\ want\ control\ over\ memory\ allocation\ you\ can\ use\ the\ dynamic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03912\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ allocator\ based\ API.\ The\ allocator\ consists\ of\ two\ callbacks\ for\ allocating}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03913\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ and\ freeing\ memory\ and\ optional\ userdata\ so\ you\ can\ plugin\ your\ own\ allocator.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03914\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03915\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ The\ final\ and\ easiest\ way\ can\ be\ used\ by\ defining}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03916\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ NK\_INCLUDE\_DEFAULT\_ALLOCATOR\ which\ uses\ the\ standard\ library\ memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03917\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ allocation\ functions\ malloc\ and\ free\ and\ takes\ over\ complete\ control\ over}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03918\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ memory\ in\ this\ library.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03919\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04038\ \textcolor{comment}{/*===============================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04039\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04040\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ TEXT\ EDITOR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04042\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ===============================================================*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04043\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Editing\ text\ in\ this\ library\ is\ handled\ by\ either\ `nk\_edit\_string`\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04044\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ `nk\_edit\_buffer`.\ But\ like\ almost\ everything\ in\ this\ library\ there\ are\ multiple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04045\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ways\ of\ doing\ it\ and\ a\ balance\ between\ control\ and\ ease\ of\ use\ with\ memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04046\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ as\ well\ as\ functionality\ controlled\ by\ flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04047\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04048\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ library\ generally\ allows\ three\ different\ levels\ of\ memory\ control:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04049\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ First\ of\ is\ the\ most\ basic\ way\ of\ just\ providing\ a\ simple\ char\ array\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04050\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ string\ length.\ This\ method\ is\ probably\ the\ easiest\ way\ of\ handling\ simple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04051\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ user\ text\ input.\ Main\ upside\ is\ complete\ control\ over\ memory\ while\ the\ biggest}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04052\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ downside\ in\ comparison\ with\ the\ other\ two\ approaches\ is\ missing\ undo/redo.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04053\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04054\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ For\ UIs\ that\ require\ undo/redo\ the\ second\ way\ was\ created.\ It\ is\ based\ on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04055\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ a\ fixed\ size\ nk\_text\_edit\ struct,\ which\ has\ an\ internal\ undo/redo\ stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04056\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ is\ mainly\ useful\ if\ you\ want\ something\ more\ like\ a\ text\ editor\ but\ don't\ want}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04057\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ to\ have\ a\ dynamically\ growing\ buffer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04058\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04059\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ final\ way\ is\ using\ a\ dynamically\ growing\ nk\_text\_edit\ struct,\ which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04060\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ has\ both\ a\ default\ version\ if\ you\ don't\ care\ where\ memory\ comes\ from\ and\ an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04061\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ allocator\ version\ if\ you\ do.\ While\ the\ text\ editor\ is\ quite\ powerful\ for\ its}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04062\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ complexity\ I\ would\ not\ recommend\ editing\ gigabytes\ of\ data\ with\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04063\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ It\ is\ rather\ designed\ for\ uses\ cases\ which\ make\ sense\ for\ a\ GUI\ library\ not\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04064\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ an\ full\ blown\ text\ editor.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04065\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04066\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ NK\_TEXTEDIT\_UNDOSTATECOUNT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04067\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ NK\_TEXTEDIT\_UNDOSTATECOUNT\ \ \ \ \ 99}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04154\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04155\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ DRAWING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04156\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04157\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ===============================================================*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04158\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ \ This\ library\ was\ designed\ to\ be\ render\ backend\ agnostic\ so\ it\ does}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04159\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ not\ draw\ anything\ to\ screen.\ Instead\ all\ drawn\ shapes,\ widgets}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04160\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ are\ made\ of,\ are\ buffered\ into\ memory\ and\ make\ up\ a\ command\ queue.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04161\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ Each\ frame\ therefore\ fills\ the\ command\ buffer\ with\ draw\ commands}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04162\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ that\ then\ need\ to\ be\ executed\ by\ the\ user\ and\ his\ own\ render\ backend.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04163\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ After\ that\ the\ command\ buffer\ needs\ to\ be\ cleared\ and\ a\ new\ frame\ can\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04164\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ started.\ It\ is\ probably\ important\ to\ note\ that\ the\ command\ buffer\ is\ the\ main}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04165\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drawing\ API\ and\ the\ optional\ vertex\ buffer\ API\ only\ takes\ this\ format\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04166\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ converts\ it\ into\ a\ hardware\ accessible\ format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04167\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04168\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ To\ use\ the\ command\ queue\ to\ draw\ your\ own\ widgets\ you\ can\ access\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04169\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ command\ buffer\ of\ each\ window\ by\ calling\ `nk\_window\_get\_canvas`\ after}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04170\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ previously\ having\ called\ `nk\_begin`:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04171\ \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04191\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04193\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04194\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ Important\ to\ know\ if\ you\ want\ to\ create\ your\ own\ widgets\ is\ the\ `nk\_widget`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04195\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ call.\ It\ allocates\ space\ on\ the\ panel\ reserved\ for\ this\ widget\ to\ be\ used,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04196\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ but\ also\ returns\ the\ state\ of\ the\ widget\ space.\ If\ your\ widget\ is\ not\ seen\ and\ does}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04197\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ not\ have\ to\ be\ updated\ it\ is\ '0'\ and\ you\ can\ just\ return.\ If\ it\ only\ has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04198\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ to\ be\ drawn\ the\ state\ will\ be\ `NK\_WIDGET\_ROM`\ otherwise\ you\ can\ do\ both}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04199\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ update\ and\ draw\ your\ widget.\ The\ reason\ for\ separating\ is\ to\ only\ draw\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04200\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ update\ what\ is\ actually\ necessary\ which\ is\ crucial\ for\ performance.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04201\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04492\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04493\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ The\ draw\ list\ is\ based\ on\ a\ path\ buffering\ and\ polygon\ and\ polyline}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04494\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ rendering\ API\ which\ allows\ a\ lot\ of\ ways\ to\ draw\ 2D\ content\ to\ screen.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04495\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ In\ fact\ it\ is\ probably\ more\ powerful\ than\ needed\ but\ allows\ even\ more\ crazy}}
